            <script type="text/javascript">
             $(function() {
  $('.navbar-nav>li').click(function() {
      // remove classes from all
      $('.navbar-nav>li').removeClass("active");
      // add class to the one we clicked
      $(this).addClass("active");
   });
});

$(function(){
    var current = location.pathname;
    $('.navbar-nav>li').each(function(){
        var navItem = $(this);
        // if the current path is like this link, make it active
        if($(this).find("a").attr('href') == current){
            navItem.addClass('active');
            var vertical = $('.navbar-nav>li.active>a').clone().children().remove().end().text();
            $("#active-vertical").text(vertical);
        }
    })
})
            </script>

     $(document).ready(function() {
           $('.custom-search-input .trigger').click(function() {
               // Hide the trigger image:
               //$(this).animate({width:0},1000);
               // At the same time slide the div open
               $('.search-query').animate({width: 'toggle'},1000, function(){
                   // This function/ code will be executed on complete:
                   //$(this).find('input')[0].focus(); // For bonus, the input will now get autofocus
               });
           });
       });

       $(window).scroll(function (event) {
           var d = $('.header-area .cbcontainer').width();
           if (d > 1139){
               var scrollPosition = $(window).scrollTop();
               if (scrollPosition > 10) {
                   if ($('.header-area #mainheader h1.cnn-life-header-label').length){
                       $('.header-area #mainheader h1.cnn-life-header-label').addClass("scroll");
                   }
               }
               else {
                   if ($('.header-area #mainheader h1.cnn-life-header-label').length) {
                       $('.header-area #mainheader h1.cnn-life-header-label').removeClass("scroll");
                   }
               }
           }else {
               if ($('.header-area #mainheader h1.cnn-life-header-label').length) {
                   $('.header-area #mainheader h1.cnn-life-header-label').removeClass("scroll");
               }
           }
           // Do something
       });
       $(window).resize(function (event) {
           var d = $('.header-area .cbcontainer').width();
           if (1139 > d ){
               if ($('.header-area #mainheader h1.cnn-life-header-label').length) {
                   $('.header-area #mainheader h1.cnn-life-header-label').removeClass("scroll");
               }
           }
       });
    </script>

         <script>
          function playVideo(videoSource, articleLink) {
$('#modal_video').toggle();
if (videoSource.indexOf("youtube") > -1){
$("#video").attr('src',videoSource + "?autoplay=1&amp;rel=0&amp;modestbranding=1&amp;showinfo=0");
} else if (videoSource.indexOf("facebook") > -1){
$("#video").attr('src',videoSource);
}
$("#article-url").attr('href', articleLink );
}
$(document).ready(function() {
// Gets the video src from the data-src on each button
/*
var $videoSrc;
$('.video-btn').click(function() {
$videoSrc = $(this).data( "src" );
$articleUrl = $(this).data( "url" );
});
console.log($videoSrc);
// when the modal is opened autoplay it
$('#modal_video').on('shown.bs.modal', function (e) {
// set the video src to autoplay and not to show related video. Youtube related video is like a box of chocolates... you never know what you're gonna get
$("#video").attr('src',$videoSrc + "?autoplay=1&amp;rel=0&amp;modestbranding=1&amp;showinfo=0");
$("#article-url").attr('href', $articleUrl );
})
*/
// stop playing the youtube video when I close the modal
$('#modal_video').on('hide.bs.modal', function (e) {
// a poor man's stop video
$("#video").attr('src',"");
$("#article-url").attr('href', "");
})
// document ready
});
         </script>

             jQuery(document).ready(function () {
var imgcontainer = $(".vplay.align-middle").find(".img-container");

            <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
             /* this block is applicable for a special feature implemented for elention 2016*/
/*adjust the position of teaser image and header*/
function adjustPosition() {
var specialTeaserObj = $(".special-teaser");
if(specialTeaserObj.length > 0) {
console.log("special teaser");
specialTeaserObj.each(function(){
var headerObj = specialTeaserObj.find(".subhead-lead-votes");
if(headerObj.length == 1) {
var headerHeight = headerObj.parent().height();
var headerParentObj = headerObj.parent();
var imgContainerObj = specialTeaserObj.find(".img-container");
var imgWidth = imgContainerObj.find("img").width();
if(imgContainerObj.length == 1) {
imgContainerObj.css("margin-top", (headerHeight-1) + "px");
headerParentObj.css("margin-bottom", "-" + headerHeight + "px");
headerParentObj.css("z-index", 11);
headerParentObj.css("width", (imgWidth + 25) + "px")
}
}
});
}
}
$(document).ready(function () {
adjustPosition();
$(window).resize(function() {
console.log("tracking resize of windows... adjusting the position of teaser image and header");
adjustPosition();
});
});
            </script>
